Accounting	O

When	O

,	O

on	O

price	O
that	O

at	O

place	O

in	O

principal	O
market	O

Accounting	O
policy	O
for	O
share-based	O
payments	O
Equity-settled	O
transactions	O
are	O
awards	O
of	O
shares	O
,	O
or	O
options	O
over	O
shares	O
,	O
that	O
are	O
provided	O
to	O
employees	O
in	O
exchange	O
for	O
the	O
rendering	O
of	O
services.	O
Cash-settled	O
transactions	O
are	O
awards	O
of	O
cash	O
for	O
the	O
exchange	O
of	O
services	O
,	O
where	O
the	O
amount	O
of	O
cash	O
is	O
determined	O
by	O
reference	O
to	O
the	O
share	O
price.	O
The	O
cost	O
of	O
equity-settled	O
transactions	O
are	O
measured	O
at	O
fair	O
value	O
on	O
grant	O
date.	O
Fair	O
value	O
is	O
independently	O
determined	O
using	O
either	O
the	O
Binomial	O
or	O
Black-Scholes	O
option	O
pricing	O
model	O
that	O
takes	O
into	O
account	O
the	O
exercise	O
price	O
,	O
the	O
term	O
of	O
the	O
option	O
,	O
the	O
impact	O
of	O
dilution	O
,	O
the	O
share	O
price	O
at	O
grant	O
date	O
and	O
expected	O
price	O
volatility	O
of	O
the	O
underlying	O
